 \n        for signature in &known_anti_cheat_signatures {\n            if driver.name.contains(signature) {\n                return true;\n            }\n        }\n        \n        false\n    }\n}\n```\n\n---\n\n## 4. Phase 2: Trusted Handshake Initiation\n\n### 4.1 Challenge-Response Protocol\n\n```\n┌─────────────────┐         ┌─────────────────┐\n│   Game/Anti-Cheat│         │    SENTINEL     │\n└─────────────────┘         └─────────────────┘\n         │                           │\n         │  1. Challenge Request      │\n         │──────────────────────────>│\n         │                           │\n         │                           │\n         │  2. Challenge Generation  │\n         │                           │\n         │  3. Digital Signature     │\n         │<──────────────────────────│\n         │                           │\n         │  4. Response Validation   │\n         │──────────────────────────>│\n         │                           │\n         │  5. Trust Establishment   │\n         │<──────────────────────────│\n```\n\n### 4.2 Cryptographic Protocol\n\n```rust\nuse ring::signature::{Ed25519, KeyPair};\nuse ring::rand::SystemRandom;\n\nstruct TrustedHandshake {\n    key_pair: Ed25519KeyPair,\n    random: SystemRandom,\n    challenge_cache: HashMap<String, Challenge>,\n}\n\nstruct Challenge {\n    nonce: [u8; 32],\n    timestamp: u64,\n    session_id: String,\n}\n\nstruct Response {\n    signature: Vec<u8>,\n    challenge_hash: [u8; 32],\n    integrity_proof: IntegrityProof,\n}\n\nimpl TrustedHandshake {\n    fn initiate_handshake(&mut self, game_id: &str) -> Challenge {\n        // Generate nonce\n        let mut nonce = [0u8; 32];\n        self.random.fill(&mut nonce).unwrap();\n        \n        let challenge = Challenge {\n            nonce,\n            timestamp: get_current_timestamp(),\n            session_id: generate_session_id(),\n        };\n        \n        // Cache challenge\n        self.challenge_cache.insert(\n            challenge.session_id.clone(),\n            challenge.clone()\n        );\n        \n        challenge\n    }\n    \n    fn sign_challenge(&self, challenge: &Challenge) -> Response {\n        // Hash challenge\n        let challenge_hash = hash_challenge(challenge);\n        \n        // Sign with private key\n        let signature = self.key_pair.sign(\n            &challenge_hash,\n            &self.random\n        );\n        \n        // Generate integrity proof\n        let integrity_proof = self.generate_integrity_proof();\n        \n        Response {\n            signature: signature.as_ref().to_vec(),\n            challenge_hash,\n            integrity_proof,\n        }\n    }\n    \n    fn verify_response(&self, response: &Response, expected_hash: [u8; 32]) -> bool {\n        // Verify challenge hash matches\n        if response.challenge_hash != expected_hash {\n            return false;\n        }\n        \n        // Verify signature\n        let public_key = self.key_pair.public_key();\n        match public_key.verify(\n            &response.challenge_hash,\n            &response.signature\n        ) {\n            Ok(()) => true,\n            Err(_) => false,\n        }\n    }\n}\n```\n\n### 4.3 Secure Key Exchange\n\n```rust\nuse ring::agreement::{agree_ephemeral, EphemeralPrivateKey, UnparsedPublicKey, X25519};\n\nstruct KeyExchange {\n    private_key: EphemeralPrivateKey<X25519>,\n    peer_public_key: Option<UnparsedPublicKey<X25519>>,\n}\n\nimpl KeyExchange {\n    fn new() -> Result<Self, Error> {\n        let rng = SystemRandom::new();\n        let private_key = EphemeralPrivateKey::generate(&rng)?;\n        \n        Ok(KeyExchange {\n            private_key,\n            peer_public_key: None,\n        })\n    }\n    \n    fn set_peer_public_key(&mut self, public_key_bytes: &[u8]) -> Result<(), Error> {\n        self.peer_public_key = Some(\n            UnparsedPublicKey::new(&X25519, public_key_bytes)?\n        );\n        Ok(())\n    }\n    \n    fn derive_shared_secret(&self) -> Result<Vec<u8>, Error> {\n        let peer_public_key = self.peer_public_key.as_ref()\n            .ok_or(Error::NoPeerPublicKey)?;\n        \n        let shared_secret = agree_ephemeral(\n            self.private_key.compute_public_key()?,\n            peer_public_key,\n            (),\n            |secret| Ok(secret.to_vec())\n        )?;\n        \n        Ok(shared_secret)\n    }\n}\n```\n\n---\n\n## 5. Phase 3: System Integrity Proof\n\n### 5.1 Secure Boot Verification\n\n```rust\nstruct SecureBootVerifier {\n    tpm: TpmDevice,\n    firmware_db: FirmwareDatabase,\n}\n\nstruct IntegrityProof {\n    secure_boot_status: bool,\n    firmware_hash: [u8; 32],\n    bootloader_hash: [u8; 32],\n    kernel_hash: [u8; 32],\n    system_files_hash: [u8; 32],\n    sentinelt_hash: [u8; 32],\n    timestamp: u64,\n}\n\nimpl SecureBootVerifier {\n    fn verify_secure_boot(&self) -> bool {\n        // Check TPM secure boot status\n        match self.tpm.get_secure_boot_status() {\n            SecureBootStatus::Enabled => true,\n            _ => false,\n        }\n    }\n    \n    fn generate_integrity_proof(&self) -> IntegrityProof {\n        // Get firmware hash\n        let firmware_hash = self.get_firmware_hash();\n        \n        // Get bootloader hash\n        let bootloader_hash = self.get_bootloader_hash();\n        \n        // Get kernel hash\n        let kernel_hash = self.get_kernel_hash();\n        \n        // Get system files hash\n        let system_files_hash = self.get_system_files_hash();\n        \n        // Get SENTINEL hash\n        let sentinelt_hash = self.get_sentinelt_hash();\n        \n        IntegrityProof {\n            secure_boot_status: self.verify_secure_boot(),\n            firmware_hash,\n            bootloader_hash,\n            kernel_hash,\n            system_files_hash,\n            sentinelt_hash,\n            timestamp: get_current_timestamp(),\n        }\n    }\n    \n    fn get_firmware_hash(&self) -> [u8; 32] {\n        // Query TPM for firmware measurements\n        let pcr_values = self.tpm.read_pcr_registers();\n        \n        // Hash the PCR values\n        hash_pcr_values(&pcr_values)\n    }\n}\n```\n\n### 5.2 TPM Attestation\n\n```rust\nuse tss_esapi::{Context, Tcti};\n\nstruct TpmAttestor {\n    context: Context,\n    ak_handle: KeyHandle, // Attestation Key\n}\n\nimpl TpmAttestor {\n    fn new() -> Result<Self, Error> {\n        let tcti = Tcti::from_environment_variable()?;\n        let context = Context::new(tcti)?;\n        \n        // Load or create attestation key\n        let ak_handle = context.load_or_create_ak()?;\n        \n        Ok(TpmAttestor {\n            context,\n            ak_handle,\n        })\n    }\n    \n    fn generate_attestation(&self, nonce: &[u8]) -> Result<Attestation, Error> {\n        // Generate attestation using TPM\n        let attestation = self.context.attest(\n            self.ak_handle,\n            nonce,\n            &[PCRTag::PCR0, PCRTag::PCR1] // Which PCRs to attest\n        )?;\n        \n        Ok(Attestation {\n            signature: attestation.signature,\n            pcr_values: attestation.pcr_values,\n            timestamp: attestation.timestamp,\n        })\n    }\n    \n    fn verify_attestation(&self, attestation: &Attestation) -> Result<bool, Error> {\n        // Verify attestation signature using AK public key\n        self.context.verify_attestation(\n            self.ak_handle,\n            attestation\n        )\n    }\n}\n```\n\n### 5.3 Hash Chain Validation\n\n```rust\nstruct HashChainValidator {\n    chain: Vec<HashEntry>,\n    merkle_tree: MerkleTree,\n}\n\nstruct HashEntry {\n    hash: [u8; 32],\n    timestamp: u64,\n    previous_hash: [u8; 32],\n    metadata: HashMap<String, String>,\n}\n\nimpl HashChainValidator {\n    fn validate_chain(&self) -> bool {\n        for (i, entry) in self.chain.iter().enumerate() {\n            // Check hash link\n            if i > 0 {\n                let prev_entry = &self.chain[i - 1];\n                if entry.previous_hash != prev_entry.hash {\n                    return false;\n                }\n            }\n            \n            // Verify hash integrity\n            let computed_hash = compute_hash(&entry.metadata);\n            if computed_hash != entry.hash {\n                return false;\n            }\n        }\n        \n        true\n    }\n    \n    fn verify_merkle_proof(&self, proof: &MerkleProof) -> bool {\n        self.merkle_tree.verify_proof(proof)\n    }\n}\n```\n\n---\n\n## 6. Phase 4: Anti-Cheat Compatibility\n\n### 6.1 Kernel Driver Whitelist\n\n```rust\nstruct KernelDriverWhitelist {\n    allowed_drivers: HashMap<String, DriverInfo>,\n    anti_cheat_compatibility: HashMap<String, CompatibilityProfile>,\n}\n\nstruct DriverInfo {\n    name: String,\n    signature_hash: [u8; 32],\n    publisher: String,\n    trust_level: TrustLevel,\n}\n\nstruct CompatibilityProfile {\n    anti_cheat_name: String,\n    compatible_drivers: Vec<String>,\n    memory_regions: Vec<MemoryRegion>,\n    allowed_behaviors: Vec<BehaviorPattern>,\n}\n\nimpl KernelDriverWhitelist {\n    fn is_compatible(&self, driver: &DriverInfo, anti_cheat: &str) -> bool {\n        if let Some(profile) = self.anti_cheat_compatibility.get(anti_cheat) {\n            // Check if driver is in compatible list\n            profile.compatible_drivers.contains(&driver.name)\n        } else {\n            // Default: only allow signed Microsoft drivers\n            driver.publisher == "Microsoft Corporation"\n        }\n    }\n    \n    fn mark_memory_region(&self, process_id: u32, region: MemoryRegion) {\n        // Mark memory region as safe for anti-cheat\n        let anti_cheat = self.detect_anti_cheat(process_id);\n        \n        if let Some(profile) = self.anti_cheat_compatibility.get(&anti_cheat) {\n            for allowed_region in &profile.memory_regions {\n                if region.overlaps(allowed_region) {\n                    region.set_safe_for_anti_cheat(true);\n                }\n            }\n        }\n    }\n}\n```\n\n### 6.2 Memory Region Marking\n\n```rust\nstruct MemoryRegion {\n    start_address: u64,\n    end_address: u64,\n    protection: MemoryProtection,\n    purpose: RegionPurpose,\n    anti_cheat_safe: bool,\n}\n\n#[derive(PartialEq)]\nenum RegionPurpose {\n    SENTINELCode,\n    SENTINELData,\n    GameCode,\n    GameData,\n    SystemCode,\n    SystemData,\n    Unknown,\n}\n\nimpl MemoryRegion {\n    fn overlaps(&self, other: &MemoryRegion) -> bool {\n        self.start_address < other.end_address &&\n        self.end_address > other.start_address\n    }\n    \n    fn set_safe_for_anti_cheat(&mut self, safe: bool) {\n        self.anti_cheat_safe = safe;\n    }\n}\n```\n\n### 6.3 Anti-Tamper Proof\n\n```rust\nstruct AntiTamperProof {\n    integrity_hash: [u8; 32],\n    signature: Vec<u8>,\n    timestamp: u64,\n    version: String,\n}\n\nimpl AntiTamperProof {\n    fn generate(&self) -> Self {\n        // Calculate integrity hash\n        let integrity_hash = calculate_integrity_hash();\n        \n        // Sign with private key\n        let signature = sign_hash(&integrity_hash);\n        \n        AntiTamperProof {\n            integrity_hash,\n            signature,\n            timestamp: get_current_timestamp(),\n            version: SENTINEL_VERSION.to_string(),\n        }\n    }\n    \n    fn verify(&self) -> bool {\n        // Verify integrity hash\n        let current_hash = calculate_integrity_hash();\n        if current_hash != self.integrity_hash {\n            return false;\n        }\n        \n        // Verify signature\n        verify_signature(&self.integrity_hash, &self.signature)\n    }\n}\n```\n\n---\n\n## 7. Phase 5: Zero-Scan Mode Activation\n\n### 7.1 Disk Scanning Suspension\n\n```rust\nstruct ScanSuspendManager {\n    scanning_active: bool,\n    gaming_active: bool,\n    pending_scan_queue: Vec<ScanTask>,\n}\n\nimpl ScanSuspendManager {\n    fn enter_gaming_mode(&mut self) {\n        self.gaming_active = true;\n        \n        // Suspend all active scans\n        self.suspend_active_scans();\n        \n        // Don\'t schedule new scans\n        self.scanning_active = false;\n    }\n    \n    fn exit_gaming_mode(&mut self) {\n        self.gaming_active = false;\n        \n        // Resume scanning\n        self.scanning_active = true;\n        \n        // Process pending scans\n        self.process_pending_scans();\n    }\n    \n    fn suspend_active_scans(&mut self) {\n        // Move active scans to pending queue\n        while let Some(scan) = self.get_active_scan() {\n            scan.suspend();\n            self.pending_scan_queue.push(scan);\n        }\n    }\n    \n    fn process_pending_scans(&mut self) {\n        // Process scans that were suspended\n        for scan in self.pending_scan_queue.drain(..) {\n            scan.resume();\n            self.schedule_scan(scan);\n        }\n    }\n}\n```\n\n### 7.2 Background Process Prioritization\n\n```rust\nuse winapi::um::processthreadsapi::SetPriorityClass;\nuse winapi::um::winnt::PROCESS_MODE_BACKGROUND_BEGIN;\n\nstruct ProcessPrioritizer {\n    background_processes: Vec<ProcessId>,\n}\n\nimpl ProcessPrioritizer {\n    fn prioritize_for_gaming(&mut self, game_process: ProcessId) {\n        // Set game process to high priority\n        unsafe {\n            SetPriorityClass(\n                game_process.handle(),\n                HIGH_PRIORITY_CLASS\n            );\n        }\n        \n        // Set background processes to low priority\n        for pid in &self.background_processes {\n            unsafe {\n                SetPriorityClass(\n                    pid.handle(),\n                    BELOW_NORMAL_PRIORITY_CLASS\n                );\n                \n                // Enable background mode\n                SetPriorityClass(\n                    pid.handle(),\n                    PROCESS_MODE_BACKGROUND_BEGIN\n                );\n            }\n        }\n    }\n    \n    fn restore_priorities(&mut self) {\n        for pid in &self.background_processes {\n            unsafe {\n                SetPriorityClass(\n                    pid.handle(),\n                    NORMAL_PRIORITY_CLASS\n                );\n                \n                // Disable background mode\n                SetPriorityClass(\n                    pid.handle(),\n                    PROCESS_MODE_BACKGROUND_END\n                );\n            }\n        }\n    }\n}\n```\n\n### 7.3 Resource Optimization\n\n```rust\nstruct ResourceOptimizer {\n    cpu_throttle_enabled: bool,\n    memory_compression_enabled: bool,\n    network_throttle_enabled: bool,\n}\n\nimpl ResourceOptimizer {\n    fn optimize_for_gaming(&mut self) {\n        // Throttle CPU usage for non-essential processes\n        self.cpu_throttle_enabled = true;\n        self.set_cpu_throttle(50.0); // 50% of normal\n        \n        // Enable memory compression\n        self.memory_compression_enabled = true;\n        self.enable_memory_compression();\n        \n        // Throttle network for non-gaming traffic\n        self.network_throttle_enabled = true;\n        self.set_network_throttle(1_000_000); // 1 Mbps\n    }\n    \n    fn restore_normal(&mut self) {\n        self.cpu_throttle_enabled = false;\n        self.set_cpu_throttle(100.0);\n        \n        self.memory_compression_enabled = false;\n        self.disable_memory_compression();\n        \n        self.network_throttle_enabled = false;\n        self.set_network_throttle(u32::MAX);\n    }\n}\n```\n\n---\n\n## 8. Phase 6: Gaming Optimization\n\n### 8.1 AI Overclocking\n\n**Concept:** AI analizuje w czasie rzeczywistym obciążenie systemu podczas gry i dynamicznie dostosowuje napięcie i taktowanie dla optymalnej wydajności.\n\n```rust\nstruct AIOverclocker {\n    gpu_controller: GpuController,\n    cpu_controller: CpuController,\n    ram_controller: RamController,\n    ai_model: OverclockingModel,\n}\n\nstruct OverclockingParameters {\n    gpu_core_clock: u32,\n    gpu_memory_clock: u32,\n    gpu_voltage: f32,\n    cpu_core_clock: u32,\n    cpu_voltage: f32,\n    ram_frequency: u32,\n    ram_timings: RamTimings,\n}\n\nimpl AIOverclocker {\n    fn optimize(&mut self, game_id: &str) -> OverclockingParameters {\n        // Monitor system load\n        let system_metrics = self.collect_metrics();\n        \n        // AI prediction for optimal settings\n        let predicted_params = self.ai_model.predict(\n            &system_metrics,\n            game_id\n        );\n        \n        // Apply settings gradually\n        self.apply_overclock(&predicted_params);\n        \n        predicted_params\n    }\n    \n    fn collect_metrics(&self) -> SystemMetrics {\n        SystemMetrics {\n            gpu_utilization: self.gpu_controller.get_utilization(),\n            gpu_temperature: self.gpu_controller.get_temperature(),\n            gpu_power_draw: self.gpu_controller.get_power_draw(),\n            \n            cpu_utilization: self.cpu_controller.get_utilization(),\n            cpu_temperature: self.cpu_controller.get_temperature(),\n            cpu_power_draw: self.cpu_controller.get_power_draw(),\n            \n            ram_utilization: self.ram_controller.get_utilization(),\n            ram_frequency: self.ram_controller.get_frequency(),\n            \n            frame_rate: self.get_frame_rate(),\n            frame_time: self.get_frame_time(),\n            \n            game_specific_metrics: self.collect_game_metrics(),\n        }\n    }\n    \n    fn apply_overclock(&mut self, params: &OverclockingParameters) {\n        // Apply GPU overclock\n        self.gpu_controller.set_core_clock(params.gpu_core_clock);\n        self.gpu_controller.set_memory_clock(params.gpu_memory_clock);\n        self.gpu_controller.set_voltage(params.gpu_voltage);\n        \n        // Apply CPU overclock\n        self.cpu_controller.set_core_clock(params.cpu_core_clock);\n        self.cpu_controller.set_voltage(params.cpu_voltage);\n        \n        // Apply RAM overclock\n        self.ram_controller.set_frequency(params.ram_frequency);\n        self.ram_controller.set_timings(params.ram_timings);\n    }\n}\n```\n\n### 8.2 AI Model for Overclocking\n\n```python\nimport torch\nimport torch.nn as nn\n\nclass OverclockingPredictor(nn.Module):\n    def __init__(self, num_features=20, num_outputs=7):\n        super().__init__()\n        \n        # Feature extraction\n        self.fc1 = nn.Linear(num_features, 64)\n        self.fc2 = nn.Linear(64, 32)\n        \n        # Temperature awareness\n        self.temp_encoder = nn.Sequential(\n            nn.Linear(3, 16),\n            nn.ReLU(),\n        )\n        \n        # Game-specific encoder\n        self.game_encoder = nn.Embedding(1000, 16)\n        \n        # Combined features\n        self.fc3 = nn.Linear(32 + 16 + 16, 64)\n        self.fc4 = nn.Linear(64, 32)\n        \n        # Output layer\n        self.fc5 = nn.Linear(32, num_outputs)\n        \n    def forward(self, features, temperatures, game_id):\n        # Extract features\n        x = torch.relu(self.fc1(features))\n        x = torch.relu(self.fc2(x))\n        \n        # Encode temperatures\n        temp = self.temp_encoder(temperatures)\n        \n        # Encode game ID\n        game = self.game_encoder(game_id)\n        \n        # Combine\n        x = torch.cat([x, temp, game], dim=-1)\n        x = torch.relu(self.fc3(x))\n        x = torch.relu(self.fc4(x))\n        \n        # Predict overclocking parameters\n        output = self.fc5(x)\n        \n        # Output format:\n        # [gpu_core_clock, gpu_mem_clock, gpu_voltage,\n        #  cpu_core_clock, cpu_voltage, ram_freq, ram_timings]\n        return output\n\n# Training\ndef train_overclocking_model():\n    model = OverclockingPredictor()\n    optimizer = torch.optim.Adam(model.parameters(), lr=0.001)\n    \n    for epoch in range(1000):\n        for batch in dataloader:\n            features, temps, game_id, optimal_params = batch\n            \n            optimizer.zero_grad()\n            predicted = model(features, temps, game_id)\n            \n            # MSE loss for regression\n            loss = nn.MSELoss()(predicted, optimal_params)\n            \n            # Add temperature penalty\n            temp_penalty = calculate_temp_penalty(predicted)\n            loss += temp_penalty\n            \n            loss.backward()\n            optimizer.step()\n    \n    return model\n```\n\n### 8.3 RAM Defolding\n\n**Concept:** Kompresja procesów tła w RAM, aby zwolnić pamięć dla gry.\n\n```rust\nstruct RamDefolder {\n    background_processes: Vec<ProcessId>,\n    compression_ratio: f64,\n}\n\nimpl RamDefolder {\n    def compress_background_processes(&mut self) {\n        for pid in &self.background_processes {\n            let process = Process::from_id(*pid);\n            \n            // Compress process memory\n            self.compress_process_memory(&process);\n            \n            // Swap out to compressed RAM\n            self.swap_to_compressed(&process);\n        }\n    }\n    \n    def compress_process_memory(&self, process: &Process) {\n        let memory_regions = process.get_memory_regions();\n        \n        for region in memory_regions {\n            if region.is_compressible() {\n                // Compress memory region\n                let compressed = self.compress_region(&region);\n                \n                // Update region with compressed data\n                region.set_compressed(compressed);\n            }\n        }\n    }\n    \n    def restore_processes(&mut self) {\n        for pid in &self.background_processes {\n            let process = Process::from_id(*pid);\n            \n            // Decompress process memory\n            self.decompress_process_memory(&process);\n            \n            // Swap back to normal RAM\n            self.swap_from_compressed(&process);\n        }\n    }\n}\n```\n\n### 8.4 Network Optimization\n\n```rust\nstruct NetworkOptimizer {\n    priority_queue: PriorityQueue<Packet>,\n    game_traffic_ports: Vec<u16>,\n}\n\nimpl NetworkOptimizer {\n    fn optimize_for_gaming(&mut self, game_ports: Vec<u16>) {\n        self.game_traffic_ports = game_ports;\n        \n        // Set high priority for game traffic\n        self.set_traffic_priority();\n    }\n    \n    fn set_traffic_priority(&self) {\n        for port in &self.game_traffic_ports {\n            // Set QoS priority for game ports\n            self.set_qos_priority(*port, Priority::High);\n        }\n        \n        // Set low priority for background traffic\n        self.set_background_priority(Priority::Low);\n    }\n    \n    fn process_packet(&mut self, packet: Packet) -> bool {\n        // Check if packet is game traffic\n        if self.game_traffic_ports.contains(&packet.destination_port) {\n            // Process immediately with high priority\n            true\n        } else {\n            // Queue for later processing\n            self.priority_queue.push(packet, Priority::Low);\n            false\n        }\n    }\n}\n```\n\n---\n\n## 9. Integration with Anti-Cheat Systems\n\n### 9.1 Supported Anti-Cheat Systems\n\n#### Vanguard (Valorant)\n**Compatibility:** High\n**Trusted Status:** ✅ Fully Trusted\n\n**Integration:**\n- Kernel driver whitelist: `vgk.sys`\n- Memory region exclusion: Vanguard-protected regions\n- Zero-scan mode: Full support\n- Network optimization: Compatible\n\n#### EasyAntiCheat (Fortnite, Apex Legends)\n**Compatibility:** High\n**Trusted Status:** ✅ Fully Trusted\n\n**Integration:**\n- Kernel driver whitelist: `EasyAntiCheat.sys`\n- Memory region exclusion: EAC-protected regions\n- Zero-scan mode: Full support\n- Network optimization: Compatible\n\n#### BattlEye (PUBG)\n**Compatibility:** High\n**Trusted Status:** ✅ Fully Trusted\n\n**Integration:**\n- Kernel driver whitelist: `BEDaisy.sys`\n- Memory region exclusion: BattlEye-protected regions\n- Zero-scan mode: Full support\n- Network optimization: Compatible\n\n#### Ricochet (Call of Duty: Warzone)\n**Compatibility:** Medium\n**Trusted Status:** ⚠️ Partial Support\n\n**Integration:**\n- Kernel driver whitelist: Limited\n- Memory region exclusion: Partial\n- Zero-scan mode: Full support\n- Network optimization: Compatible\n\n**Limitations:**\n- Some kernel-level monitoring may trigger alerts\n- Manual whitelisting required\n- May require periodic re-verification\n\n---\n\n## 10. Teraz stworzę specyfikację RAM Defolding Mechanism.\n\n<function_calls>\n<create-file file_path="sentinel_gaming_ram_defolding.md">\n# SENTINEL - RAM Defolding Mechanism\n## Gaming Optimization Features - Phase 3.3\n\n---\n\n## 1. Wprowadzenie\n\n### Problem\nPodczas grania w nowoczesne gry, system zużywa duże ilości pamięci RAM:\n- **AAA Games:** 12-16GB RAM (wymagane)\n- **Background Processes:** 2-4GB RAM\n- **Operating System:** 2-3GB RAM\n- **Total Needed:** 16-23GB RAM\n\nUżytkownicy z 16GB RAM doświadczają:\n- Stuttering przy loading screens\n- Lags gdy gra wymaga więcej RAM\n- Page file swapping na dysku\n- Niższe FPS przy scenach z dużą ilością obiektów\n\n### Solution: RAM Defolding Mechanism\n\nRAM Defolding to inteligentny system kompresji i zarządzania pamięcią, który:\n- **Kompresuje procesy tła** w czasie rzeczywistym\n- **Zwalnia RAM** dla gry\n- **Eliminuje page file swapping**\n- **Zwiększa wydajność** gier\n- **Minimalizuje wpływ** na procesy tła\n\n---\n\n## 2. Architektura RAM Defolding\n\n### 2.1 High-Level Architecture\n\n```\n┌─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────┐\n│              RAM Defolding Manager                       │\n│                                                           │\n│  ┌─────────────────────────────────────────────────┐  │\n│  │  1. Process Monitoring                         │  │\n│  │     - Real-time RAM usage tracking             │  │\n│  │     - Process categorization                   │  │\n│  │     - Priority assignment                      │  │\n│  └─────────────────────────────────────────────────┘  │\n│                        ↓                                │\n│  ┌─────────────────────────────────────────────────┐  │\n│  │  2. Compression Engine                         │  │\n│  │     - Memory region analysis                   │  │\n│  │     - Compression algorithm selection          │  │\n│  │     - Real-time compression                    │  │\n│  └─────────────────────────────────────────────────┘  │\n│                        ↓                                │\n│  ┌─────────────────────────────────────────────────┐  │\n│  │  3. Memory Management                          │  │\n│  │     - Virtual memory allocation                │  │\n│  │     - Compression buffer management            │  │\n│  │     - Decompression on demand                  │  │\n│  └─────────────────────────────────────────────────┘  │\n│                        ↓                                │\n│  ┌─────────────────────────────────────────────────┐  │\n│  │  4. Swap Optimization                          │  │\n│  │     - Intelligent page selection               │  │\n│  │     - Pre-fetch optimization                   │  │\n│  │     - Cache management                         │  │\n│  └─────────────────────────────────────────────────┘  │\n└─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────┘\n```\n\n---\n\n## 3. Process Monitoring\n\n### 3.1 Process Categorization\n\n```rust\nuse std::collections::HashMap;\n\nstruct ProcessMonitor {\n    processes: HashMap<u32, ProcessInfo>,\n    categories: HashMap<u32, ProcessCategory>,\n    priorities: HashMap<u32, ProcessPriority>,\n}\n\n#[derive(Clone, Copy, PartialEq)]\nenum ProcessCategory {\n    Gaming,        // Priority: Highest - Never compress\n    System,        // Priority: High - Minimal compression\n    Critical,      // Priority: High - Light compression\n    Normal,        // Priority: Medium - Moderate compression\n    Background,    // Priority: Low - Aggressive compression\n    Idle,          // Priority: Lowest - Maximum compression\n}\n\n#[derive(Clone, Copy, PartialEq, PartialOrd)]\nenum ProcessPriority {\n    Critical = 5,\n    High = 4,\n    Medium = 3,\n    Low = 2,\n    Lowest = 1,\n}\n\nstruct ProcessInfo {\n    pid: u32,\n    name: String,\n    memory_usage: u64,\n    cpu_usage: f32,\n    last_active: u64,\n    category: ProcessCategory,\n    priority: ProcessPriority,\n}\n\nimpl ProcessMonitor {\n    fn categorize_process(&mut self, process: &Process) -> ProcessCategory {\n        let name = process.name().to_lowercase();\n        \n        // Gaming processes - never compress\n        if self.is_gaming_process(&name) {\n            return ProcessCategory::Gaming;\n        }\n        \n        // System processes - minimal compression\n        if self.is_system_process(&name) {\n            return ProcessCategory::System;\n        }\n        \n        // Critical processes - light compression\n        if self.is_critical_process(&name) {\n            return ProcessCategory::Critical;\n        }\n        \n        // Normal processes - moderate compression\n        if process.cpu_usage() > 5.0 {\n            return ProcessCategory::Normal;\n        }\n        \n        // Background processes - aggressive compression\n        if process.last_active() > 300_000 { // 5 minutes\n            return ProcessCategory::Idle;\n        }\n        \n        ProcessCategory::Background\n    }\n    \n    fn is_gaming_process(&self, name: &str) -> bool {\n        let gaming_processes = [\n            "valorant", "fortnite", "apex", "pubg", "csgo",\n            "dota2", "lol", "league", "minecraft", "roblox",\n            "warzone", "cod", "battlefield", "fifa", "nba2k",\n        ];\n        \n        gaming_processes.iter().any(|gp| name.contains(gp))\n    }\n    \n    fn is_system_process(&self, name: &str) -> bool {\n        let system_processes = [\n            "system", "kernel", "dwm", "explorer", "svchost",\n            "services", "lsass", "wininit", "csrss", "smss",\n        ];\n        \n        system_processes.iter().any(|sp| name.contains(sp))\n    }\n    \n    fn is_critical_process(&self, name: &str) -> bool {\n        let critical_processes = [\n            "sentinel", "security", "antivirus", "firewall",\n            "vpn", "proxy", "network", "audio", "display",\n        ];\n        \n        critical_processes.iter().any(|cp| name.contains(cp))\n    }\n    \n    fn assign_priority(&self, category: ProcessCategory) -> ProcessPriority {\n        match category {\n            ProcessCategory::Gaming => ProcessPriority::Critical,\n            ProcessCategory::System => ProcessPriority::High,\n            ProcessCategory::Critical => ProcessPriority::High,\n            ProcessCategory::Normal => ProcessPriority::Medium,\n            ProcessCategory::Background => ProcessPriority::Low,\n            ProcessCategory::Idle => ProcessPriority::Lowest,\n        }\n    }\n}\n```\n\n### 3.2 Real-Time Monitoring\n\n```rust\nimpl ProcessMonitor {\n    fn monitor_processes(&mut self, game_pid: u32) {\n        loop {\n            // Get all processes\n            let processes = self.get_all_processes();\n            \n            for process in processes {\n                let pid = process.pid();\n                \n                // Skip game process\n                if pid == game_pid {\n                    continue;\n                }\n                \n                // Categorize process\n                let category = self.categorize_process(&process);\n                let priority = self.assign_priority(category);\n                \n                // Update process info\n                self.processes.insert(pid, ProcessInfo {\n                    pid,\n                    name: process.name().to_string(),\n                    memory_usage: process.memory_usage(),\n                    cpu_usage: process.cpu_usage(),\n                    last_active: get_current_time(),\n                    category,\n                    priority,\n                });\n            }\n            \n            // Check for compression candidates\n            self.check_compression_candidates();\n            \n            // Sleep for 1 second\n            std::thread::sleep(std::time::Duration::from_secs(1));\n        }\n    }\n    \n    fn check_compression_candidates(&self) {\n        // Sort processes by priority and memory usage\n        let mut candidates: Vec<_> = self.processes.values()\n            .filter(|p| p.category != ProcessCategory::Gaming)\n            .collect();\n        \n        candidates.sort_by(|a, b| {\n            a.priority.cmp(&b.priority)\n                .then(b.memory_usage.cmp(&a.memory_usage))\n        });\n        \n        // Select top candidates for compression\n        let compression_budget = 4 * 1024 * 1024 * 1024; // 4GB\n        let mut allocated = 0;\n        \n        for process in candidates {\n            if allocated >= compression_budget {\n                break;\n            }\n            \n            if process.category == ProcessCategory::Background ||\n               process.category == ProcessCategory::Idle {\n                // Mark for compression\n                self.mark_for_compression(process.pid);\n                allocated += process.memory_usage;\n            }\n        }\n    }\n}\n```\n\n---\n\n## 4. Compression Engine\n\n### 4.1 Memory Region Analysis\n\n```rust\nstruct CompressionEngine {\n    compressors: HashMap<CompressionType, Box<dyn Compressor>>,\n}\n\n#[derive(Clone, Copy, PartialEq)]\nenum CompressionType {\n    LZ4,      // Fast, low compression\n    ZSTD,     // Balanced\n    LZMA2,    // Slow, high compression\n    Brotli,   // Text optimization\n}\n\ntrait Compressor {\n    fn compress(&self, data: &[u8]) -> Result<Vec<u8>, Error>;\n    fn decompress(&self, data: &[u8]) -> Result<Vec<u8>, Error>;\n    fn compression_ratio(&self) -> f64;\n    fn compression_speed(&self) -> f64; // MB/s\n}\n\nimpl CompressionEngine {\n    fn analyze_memory_region(&self, region: &MemoryRegion) -> CompressionRecommendation {\n        // Analyze region characteristics\n        let characteristics = self.analyze_characteristics(region);\n        \n        // Select compression type based on characteristics\n        let compression_type = self.select_compression_type(&characteristics);\n        \n        // Estimate compression ratio\n        let estimated_ratio = self.estimate_compression_ratio(\n            region,\n            compression_type\n        );\n        \n        CompressionRecommendation {\n            compression_type,\n            estimated_ratio,\n            priority: self.calculate_priority(region),\n        }\n    }\n    \n    fn analyze_characteristics(&self, region: &MemoryRegion) -> RegionCharacteristics {\n        // Sample memory region\n        let sample_size = 4096; // 4KB sample\n        let sample = region.read_sample(sample_size);\n        \n        // Calculate entropy\n        let entropy = self.calculate_entropy(&sample);\n        \n        // Detect patterns\n        let patterns = self.detect_patterns(&sample);\n        \n        // Check for compressibility\n        let compressibility = self.check_compressibility(&sample);\n        \n        RegionCharacteristics {\n            entropy,\n            patterns,\n            compressibility,\n            data_type: self.detect_data_type(&sample),\n        }\n    }\n    \n    fn select_compression_type(&self, characteristics: &RegionCharacteristics) -> CompressionType {\n        match characteristics.data_type {\n            DataType::Executable => CompressionType::LZ4,      // Fast\n            DataType::Text => CompressionType::Brotli,         // Best for text\n            DataType::Compressed => CompressionType::LZ4,      // Skip\n            DataType::Structured => CompressionType::ZSTD,     // Balanced\n            DataType::Random => CompressionType::LZ4,          // Low entropy\n            DataType::Image => CompressionType::ZSTD,          // Good balance\n        }\n    }\n    \n    fn calculate_entropy(&self, data: &[u8]) -> f64 {\n        let mut freq = [0u32; 256];\n        for &byte in data {\n            freq[byte as usize] += 1;\n        }\n        \n        let len = data.len() as f64;\n        let mut entropy = 0.0;\n        \n        for &count in &freq {\n            if count > 0 {\n                let p = count as f64 / len;\n                entropy -= p * p.log2();\n            }\n        }\n        \n        entropy\n    }\n    \n    fn check_compressibility(&self, data: &[u8]) -> f64 {\n        // Try LZ4 on sample\n        let compressed = self.compressors.get(&CompressionType::LZ4)\n            .unwrap()\n            .compress(data)\n            .unwrap();\n        \n        let ratio = data.len() as f64 / compressed.len() as f64;\n        ratio\n    }\n}\n```\n\n### 4.2 Real-Time Compression\n\n```rust\nimpl CompressionEngine {\n    fn compress_process(&self, pid: u32) -> Result<CompressionResult, Error> {\n        let process = Process::from_pid(pid)?;\n        let memory_regions = process.get_memory_regions();\n        \n        let mut compressed_regions = Vec::new();\n        let mut total_savings = 0;\n        \n        for region in memory_regions {\n            // Analyze region\n            let recommendation = self.analyze_memory_region(&region);\n            \n            // Skip if not compressible\n            if recommendation.estimated_ratio < 1.5 {\n                continue;\n            }\n            \n            // Compress region\n            let compressor = self.compressors.get(&recommendation.compression_type)\n                .unwrap();\n            \n            let data = region.read_all()?;\n            let compressed = compressor.compress(&data)?;\n            \n            // Calculate savings\n            let savings = data.len() - compressed.len();\n            total_savings += savings;\n            \n            compressed_regions.push(CompressedRegion {\n                original_address: region.start_address(),\n                original_size: data.len(),\n                compressed_data: compressed,\n                compression_type: recommendation.compression_type,\n                decompression_needed: false,\n            });\n        }\n        \n        Ok(CompressionResult {\n            pid,\n            compressed_regions,\n            total_savings,\n            compression_time: get_current_time(),\n        })\n    }\n    \n    fn decompress_region(&self, compressed_region: &CompressedRegion) -> Result<Vec<u8>, Error> {\n        let compressor = self.compressors.get(&compressed_region.compression_type)\n            .unwrap();\n        \n        compressor.decompress(&compressed_region.compressed_data)\n    }\n}\n```\n\n---\n\n## 5. Memory Management\n\n### 5.1 Virtual Memory Allocation\n\n```rust\nstruct MemoryManager {\n    compressed_memory: Vec<CompressedMemoryBlock>,\n    compression_buffer: Vec<u8>,\n    max_buffer_size: usize,\n}\n\nstruct CompressedMemoryBlock {\n    original_pid: u32,\n    original_address: u64,\n    original_size: usize,\n    compressed_data: Vec<u8>,\n    compression_type: CompressionType,\n    access_count: u32,\n    last_access: u64,\n}\n\nimpl MemoryManager {\n    fn new() -> Self {\n        MemoryManager {\n            compressed_memory: Vec::new(),\n            compression_buffer: Vec::with_capacity(2 * 1024 * 1024 * 1024), // 2GB\n            max_buffer_size: 2 * 1024 * 1024 * 1024,\n        }\n    }\n    \n    fn allocate_compressed_memory(&mut self, block: CompressedMemoryBlock) -> Result<(), Error> {\n        // Check buffer space\n        if self.compression_buffer.len() + block.compressed_data.len() > self.max_buffer_size {\n            // Evict least recently used blocks\n            self.evict_lru_blocks()?;\n        }\n        \n        // Store compressed block\n        self.compressed_memory.push(block);\n        \n        Ok(())\n    }\n    \n    fn evict_lru_blocks(&mut self) -> Result<(), Error> {\n        // Sort by last access\n        self.compressed_memory.sort_by(|a, b| {\n            a.last_access.cmp(&b.last_access)\n        });\n        \n        // Evict 10% of blocks\n        let evict_count = self.compressed_memory.len() / 10;\n        let freed_space: usize = self.compressed_memory.iter()\n            .take(evict_count)\n            .map(|b| b.compressed_data.len())\n            .sum();\n        \n        self.compressed_memory.drain(0..evict_count);\n        \n        Ok(())\n    }\n    \n    fn get_compressed_block(&mut self, pid: u32, address: u64) -> Option<&CompressedMemoryBlock> {\n        self.compressed_memory.iter()\n            .find(|b| b.original_pid == pid && b.original_address == address)\n    }\n    \n    fn update_access(&mut self, pid: u32, address: u64) {\n        if let Some(block) = self.compressed_memory.iter_mut()\n            .find(|b| b.original_pid == pid && b.original_address == address) {\n            block.access_count += 1;\n            block.last_access = get_current_time();\n        }\n    }\n}\n```\n\n### 5.2 On-Demand Decompression\n\n```rust\nimpl MemoryManager {\n    fn decompress_on_demand(&mut self, pid: u32, address: u64, size: usize) -> Result<Vec<u8>, Error> {\n        // Find compressed block\n        let block = self.get_compressed_block(pid, address)\n            .ok_or(Error::BlockNotFound)?;\n        \n        // Decompress data\n        let compressor = CompressionEngine::new();\n        let decompressed = compressor.decompress_block(block)?;\n        \n        // Update access statistics\n        self.update_access(pid, address);\n        \n        Ok(decompressed)\n    }\n    \n    fn page_fault_handler(&mut self, fault_address: u64, pid: u32) -> Result<(), Error> {\n        // Find compressed region containing fault address\n        let compressed_block = self.compressed_memory.iter()\n            .find(|b| {\n                b.original_pid == pid &&\n                fault_address >= b.original_address &&\n                fault_address < b.original_address + b.original_size as u64\n            })\n            .ok_or(Error::BlockNotFound)?;\n        \n        // Decompress entire region\n        let decompressed = self.decompress_block(compressed_block)?;\n        \n        // Write decompressed data back to process memory\n        let process = Process::from_pid(pid)?;\n        process.write_memory(compressed_block.original_address, &decompressed)?;\n        \n        // Remove from compressed memory\n        let index = self.compressed_memory.iter()\n            .position(|b| b.original_address == compressed_block.original_address)\n            .unwrap();\n        self.compressed_memory.remove(index);\n        \n        Ok(())\n    }\n}\n```\n\n---\n\n## 6. Swap Optimization\n\n### 6.1 Intelligent Page Selection\n\n```rust\nstruct SwapOptimizer {\n    swap_candidates: Vec<SwapCandidate>,\n    swap_threshold: f64, // MB/s swap rate threshold\n}\n\nstruct SwapCandidate {\n    pid: u32,\n    memory_size: u64,\n    access_frequency: f64,\n    last_access: u64,\n    importance: Importance,\n}\n\n#[derive(Clone, Copy, PartialEq, PartialOrd)]\nenum Importance {\n    Critical = 4,\n    High = 3,\n    Medium = 2,\n    Low = 1,\n}\n\nimpl SwapOptimizer {\n    fn select_pages_for_swap(&mut self) -> Vec<SwapCandidate> {\n        // Calculate swap score for each candidate\n        for candidate in &mut self.swap_candidates {\n            candidate.calculate_swap_score();\n        }\n        \n        // Sort by swap score (lower = better for swap)\n        self.swap_candidates.sort_by(|a, b| {\n            a.swap_score.partial_cmp(&b.swap_score).unwrap()\n        });\n        \n        // Select top candidates\n        let swap_budget = 2 * 1024 * 1024 * 1024; // 2GB\n        let mut selected = Vec::new();\n        let mut allocated = 0;\n        \n        for candidate in &self.swap_candidates {\n            if allocated >= swap_budget {\n                break;\n            }\n            \n            if candidate.importance < Importance::High {\n                selected.push(candidate.clone());\n                allocated += candidate.memory_size;\n            }\n        }\n        \n        selected\n    }\n}\n\nimpl SwapCandidate {\n    fn calculate_swap_score(&mut self) {\n        let age_factor = (get_current_time() - self.last_access) as f64 / 60.0; // minutes\n        let access_factor = 1.0 / (self.access_frequency + 1.0);\n        let importance_factor = self.importance as u64 as f64;\n        \n        self.swap_score = age_factor * access_factor * importance_factor;\n    }\n}\n```\n\n### 6.2 Pre-Fetch Optimization\n\n```rust\nimpl SwapOptimizer {\n    fn prefetch_compressed_data(&mut self, predicted_accesses: Vec<PredictedAccess>) {\n        for access in predicted_accesses {\n            // Check if data is compressed\n            if let Some(compressed_block) = self.memory_manager\n                .get_compressed_block(access.pid, access.address) {\n                \n                // Pre-decompress to cache\n                let decompressed = self.decompress_block(compressed_block);\n                \n                // Store in pre-fetch cache\n                self.prefetch_cache.insert(access, decompressed);\n            }\n        }\n    }\n    \n    fn predict_accesses(&self, process: &Process) -> Vec<PredictedAccess> {\n        let mut predictions = Vec::new();\n        \n        // Analyze recent access patterns\n        let recent_accesses = self.get_recent_accesses(process.pid());\n        \n        // Look for sequential patterns\n        let sequential = self.detect_sequential_pattern(&recent_accesses);\n        if let Some(pattern) = sequential {\n            predictions.extend(self.extrapolate_sequence(pattern));\n        }\n        \n        // Look for strided patterns\n        let strided = self.detect_strided_pattern(&recent_accesses);\n        if let Some(pattern) = strided {\n            predictions.extend(self.extrapolate_stride(pattern));\n        }\n        \n        predictions\n    }\n}\n```\n\n---\n\n## 7. Integration with Other SENTINEL Features\n\n### 10.1 Integration with Trusted Handshake\n\n```rust\nstruct IntegratedGamingManager {\n    trusted_handshake: TrustedHandshakeManager,\n    ram_defolder: RamDefoldingManager,\n    ai_overclocker: AIOverclocker,\n}\n\nimpl IntegratedGamingManager {\n    fn enter_gaming_mode(&mut self, game_id: &str) {\n        // Initialize trusted handshake\n        self.trusted_handshake.initiate(game_id);\n        \n        // Activate RAM defolding\n        let memory_savings = self.ram_defolder.activate(game_id);\n        \n        // Start AI overclocking\n        self.ai_overclocker.optimize(game_id);\n        \n        // Send notification\n        send_notification(format!(\n            "🎮 Gaming Mode Active: {}FPS boost, {}GB RAM freed",\n            self.ai_overclocker.fps_boost(),\n            memory_savings / (1024 * 1024 * 1024)\n        ));\n    }\n    \n    fn exit_gaming_mode(&mut self) {\n        // Restore RAM\n        self.ram_defolder.deactivate();\n        \n        // Stop overclocking\n        self.ai_overclocker.restore();\n        \n        // Exit trusted handshake\n        self.trusted_handshake.terminate();\n    }\n}\n```\n\n### 10.2 Integration with NPU Offloading\n\n```rust\nimpl CompressionEngine {\n    fn compress_with_npu(&self, data: &[u8]) -> Result<Vec<u8>, Error> {\n        if self.has_npu_acceleration() {\n            // Offload compression to NPU\n            let npu = self.get_npu();\n            \n            // Transfer data to NPU\n            let npu_buffer = npu.allocate_buffer(data.len());\n            npu_buffer.copy_from(data);\n            \n            // Compress on NPU\n            let compressed = npu.compress(npu_buffer, CompressionType::ZSTD);\n            \n            // Transfer back to CPU\n            Ok(compressed.to_cpu())\n        } else {\n            // Fall back to CPU compression\n            self.compress_cpu(data)\n        }\n    }\n}\n```\n\n---\n\n## 11.
